VOCO does not yet have an official Chinese name, and the folk translation is "Voco". It was "holiday" before the hotel was rebranded and renovated. During the HI period, I stayed here too many times, and each time they upgraded me to a suite. I really loved the quaint Lingnan style and the bustling market outside the window. In "Fortress Besieged", when Fang Hongjian and Sun Roujia went to Hong Kong to visit Zhao Xinmei, they stayed in this kind of Republican-style hotel, Daai. Now after changing the cards, there are no upgrades at all, which is really sad.‚Äã‚Äã

The gym and swimming pool of Guangzhou VOCO are on the top floor. The white architectural style makes people feel like they are in another world, as if they are on a small island in Greece. It is extremely comfortable. This is the core old city of Liwan District among the eleven districts in Guangzhou. The neon night scene and the surrounding old Guangfu alleys at night are mesmerizing. It is especially suitable for first-time visitors to Guangdong or foreign tourists. The minibar is free, the welcome fruit plate is exquisitely arranged, and soup is provided in the evening. Similar to Guangzhou Center CP, it will be thoughtfully packed in an old-fashioned thermos cup. The turndown service was a mess. Apart from folding the bedding, they did not do anything else, such as cleaning the room, replenishing supplies, etc. The housekeeping staff really lowered the quality and level of the hotel. Eheng's positioning is higher than that of Zhixuan and lower than that of Holiday. Therefore, Zhixuan, Eheng and Zhixuan do not have turndown service in principle. However, as a trendy lifestyle brand, although VOCO's positioning is lower than CP, it is If it is slightly higher than a holiday, there should be a complete turndown service. You cannot use environmental protection as a shield for everything. This is unfair to guests with different needs.‚Äã‚Äã

VOCO in Wuhan has an executive lounge, but Guangzhou does not. In addition, I was not given a 60 yuan meal coupon. Among the ten InterContinental hotels in Guangzhou, the TVs in many of them only have Phoenix Chinese but no Phoenix News. The same is true for this VOCO. When I went to the lobby bar to exchange for a welcome drink, an employee (the lobby bar employees are part-time employees at the Chinese restaurant, in other words, there is no fixed staff on duty at the lobby bar) said: "VOCO also belongs to the Holiday Inn Group!" I almost missed it at that time! I'm not really happy. Staff training needs to be strengthened. The quality and design of the accompanying coffee paper cup is second only to Haixinsha Indigo. This is similar to the chairs at Nanhu Holiday, which are good places to hide dirt and evil, haha. The drainage in the bathroom is not smooth, and the water is all over the place after just a few washes.
